+  fourth_sextant_notes String[]
+  fifth_sextant        Int?
+  fifth_sextant_notes  String[]
+  sixth_sextant        Int?
+  sixth_sextant_notes  String[]
+  //Usefull - information
+  createdAt            DateTime  @default(now())
+  updatedAt            DateTime  @updatedAt
+  what_was_updated     String[]
+}

+  odontogram                         Odontogram @relation(fields: [odontogram_id], references: [id])
+  odontogram_id                      String
+  abscent                            Boolean
+  notes                              String?

+  medial_vestibular_lci              Float?
+  medial_vestibular_probing_bleeding Boolean?

+  distal_vestibular_depth            Float?

+  distal_vestibular_lci              Float?

+  mesial_lingual_lci              Float?
+  mesial_lingual_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+

+  medial_lingual_gmh              Float?
+  medial_lingual_lci              Float?
+  medial_lingual_probing_bleeding Boolean?
+
+  distal_lingual_depth            Float?
+  distal_lingual_gmh              Float?
+  distal_lingual_lci              Float?
+  distal_lingual_probing_bleeding Boolean?

+  higid                           Boolean?
+  vestibular_biofilm              Boolean?
+  palatin_biofilm                 Boolean?
+  oclusal_biofilm                 Boolean?

+  if_yes_what_type_of_restoration Restorations_types?
+  caries_white_spot_lesion        Boolean?
+  if_yes_where_white_lesion       String?

+  inative_carie                   Boolean?
+  cavity_caries_lesion            Boolean?

+  dentin_fissure                  Boolean?
+  if_yes_fissure_direction        String?

+  dental_abfraction               Boolean?
+  dental_atriction                Boolean?
+  dental_abrasion                 Boolean?
+  dental_anomaly                  Boolean?
+  if_yes_anomaly_description      String?

+  initial_radiograph              Boolean?
+  final_radiograph                Boolean?
+  pulp_status                     Pulp_states?
+  canal_calcifications            Boolean?
+  atresic_pulp_chamber            Boolean?
+  canal_depth_probing             Boolean?
+
+  canal_depth_in_mm Float? @default(26)
+
+  number_of_roots              Int?     @default(1)
+  number_of_canals             Int?     @default(1)
+  acessory_canal               Boolean?
+  lateral_canal                Boolean?

+model Anamnesis {
+  id                           String                        @id @default(cuid())
+  anamnesis_type               Questionnaires[]
+  // Personal Information
+  patient                      Patient                       @relation(fields: [patient_id], references: [id])
+  patient_id                   String
+  last_dentist_visit           DateTime
+  last_procedure               DateTime
+  what_was_done                String?
+  treatment_is_planed          Boolean                       @default(false)
+  What_treatment_is_planed     String?
+  // Personal Information
+  main_anamnesis_questionnaire Main_anamnesis_questionnaire?
+  vital_signs_questionnaire    Vital_signs_questionnaire?
+  oral_health_questionnaire    Oral_health_questionnaire?
+  createdAt                    DateTime                      @default(now())
+  updatedAt                    DateTime                      @updatedAt
+  what_was_updated             String[]
+  Diet_questionnaire           Diet_questionnaire[]
+}

+model Implantology {
+  id                                        String                     @id @default(cuid())
+  patient                                   Patient                    @relation(fields: [patient_id], references: [id])
+  patient_id                                String
+  implantology_questionnaire                Implantology_questionnaire
+  professional                              Dentist                  @relation(fields: [professional_ids], references: [id])
+  professional_ids                          String
+  implant_type                              Implant_types
+  if_type_unitary_dental_units_reabilited   String[]
+  if_type_multiple_instaled_implants_number Int?

+model Dentist {
+  id                      String                   @id @default(uuid())
+  CRO_number              String                   @unique
+  firstname               String
+  lastname                String
+  username                String                   @default(cuid())
+  password                String                   @default(cuid())
+  contactmeans            Contact_means?
+  schedule                Schedule?
+  cellphone_number        String?
+  clinic                  Clinic                   @relation("Clinic_relation", fields: [clinic_id], references: [registered_id])
+  clinic_id               String
+  email                   Email[]
+  active                  Boolean                  @default(true)
+  specialization          Clinic_specializations[]
+  ortodontics_treatments  Ortodontics?
+  implantology_treatments Implantology?
+  commission              Float?
+  patients                Patient[]                @relation(references: [id])
+  createdAt               DateTime                 @default(now())
+  updatedAt               DateTime                 @updatedAt
+  role                    String                   @default("DENTIST")
+
+  Clinic              Clinic?               @relation(fields: [clinicRegistered_id], references: [registered_id])
+  clinicRegistered_id String?
+  Email               Email[]               @relation("Dentist_relation")
+  Treatment_evolution Treatment_evolution[]
+}
+
+model Clinic_specializations {

+  specialization Specializations

+  dentistId      String?

+}

+model Employer {
